# <a name="search-the-audit-log-in-the-security--compliance-center"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-103">在安全与合规中心搜索审核日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-103">Search the audit log in the Security & Compliance Center</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-104">需要了解用户是否查看了特定文档或从其邮箱中清除了某项？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-104">Need to find if a user viewed a specific document or purged an item from their mailbox?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-105">如果是，可以使用安全与合规中心搜索统一的审核日志，以查看组织中的用户和管理员活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-105">If so, you can use the Security & Compliance Center to search the unified audit log to view user and administrator activity in your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-106">为什么是统一的审核日志？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-106">Why a unified audit log?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-107">因为你可以在 Office 365 中搜索以下类型的[用户和管理员活动](#audited-activities)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-107">Because you can search for the following types of [user and admin activity](#audited-activities) in Office 365:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-108">SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的用户活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-108">User activity in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-109">Exchange Online 中的用户活动（Exchange 邮箱审核日志记录）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-109">User activity in Exchange Online (Exchange mailbox audit logging)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-110">SharePoint Online 中的管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-110">Admin activity in SharePoint Online</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-111">Azure Active Directory 中的管理员活动（Office 365 的目录服务）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-111">Admin activity in Azure Active Directory (the directory service for Office 365)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-112">Exchange Online 中的管理员活动（Exchange 管理员审核日志记录）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-112">Admin activity in Exchange Online (Exchange admin audit logging)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-113">Sway 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-113">User and admin activity in Sway</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-114">安全与合规中心中的电子数据展示活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-114">eDiscovery activities in the security and compliance center</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-115">Power BI 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-115">User and admin activity in Power BI</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-116">Microsoft Teams 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-116">User and admin activity in Microsoft Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-117">Dynamics 365 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-117">User and admin activity in Dynamics 365</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-118">Yammer 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-118">User and admin activity in Yammer</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-119">Microsoft Power Automate 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-119">User and admin activity in Microsoft Power Automate</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-120">Microsoft Stream 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-120">User and admin activity in Microsoft Stream</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-121">Microsoft 工作区分析中的分析员和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-121">Analyst and admin activity in Microsoft Workplace Analytics</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-122">Microsoft Power Apps 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-122">User and admin activity in Microsoft Power Apps</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-123">Microsoft Forms 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-123">User and admin activity in Microsoft Forms</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-124">使用 SharePoint Online 或 Microsoft Teams 的网站的敏感度标签的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-124">User and admin activity for sensitivity labels for sites that use SharePoint Online or Microsoft Teams</span></span>

## <a name="requirements-to-search-the-audit-log"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-125">搜索审核日志的要求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-125">Requirements to search the audit log</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-126">在开始搜索审核日志之前，请务必阅读以下各项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-126">Be sure to read the following items before you start searching the audit log.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-127">你（或其他管理员）必须首先开启审核日志记录，然后才能开始搜索审核日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-127">You (or another admin) must first turn on audit logging before you can start searching the audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-128">若要将其打开，请单击安全与合规中心中**审核日志搜索**页面上的**打开审核**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-128">To turn it on, click **Turn on auditing** on the **Audit log search** page in the Security & Compliance Center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-129">（如果未看到此链接，则已为你的组织开启审核。）打开后，将显示一条消息，称正在准备审核日志，你可以在准备完成后数小时内运行搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-129">(If you don't see this link, auditing has already been turned on for your organization.) After you turn it on, a message is displayed that says the audit log is being prepared and that you can run a search in a couple of hours after the preparation is complete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-130">只需执行一次此操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-130">You only have to do this once.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-131">有关详细信息，请参阅[打开或关闭审核日志搜索](turn-audit-log-search-on-or-off.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-131">For more information, see [Turn audit log search on or off](turn-audit-log-search-on-or-off.md).</span></span>

  > [!NOTE]
  > <span data-ttu-id="85d61-132">默认正在启用审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-132">We're in the process of turning on auditing by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-133">在这之前，可以按上文所述启用审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-133">Until then, you can turn it on as previously described.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-134">必须分配有 Exchange Online 中的“仅供查看审核日志”或“审核日志”角色才能搜索审核日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-134">You have to be assigned the View-Only Audit Logs or Audit Logs role in Exchange Online to search the audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-135">默认情况下，在 Exchange 管理中心中的“**权限**”页上将这些角色分配给“合规性管理”和“组织管理”角色组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-135">By default, these roles are assigned to the Compliance Management and Organization Management role groups on the **Permissions** page in the Exchange admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-136">请注意，Office 365 和 Microsoft 365 中的全局管理员将自动添加为 Exchange Online 的组织管理角色组成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-136">Note global administrators in Office 365 and Microsoft 365 are automatically added as members of the Organization Management role group in Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-137">若要让用户能够使用最低权限级别搜索审核日志，可以在 Exchange Online 中创建自定义角色组，添加“仅供查看审核日志”或“审核日志”角色，然后将用户添加为新角色组的成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-137">To give a user the ability to search the audit log with the minimum level of privileges, you can create a custom role group in Exchange Online, add the View-Only Audit Logs or Audit Logs role, and then add the user as a member of the new role group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-138">有关详细信息，请参阅[在 Exchange Online 中管理角色组](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=730688)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-138">For more information, see [Manage role groups in Exchange Online](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=730688).</span></span>

  > [!IMPORTANT]
  > <span data-ttu-id="85d61-139">如果在安全与合规中心中的“权限”\*\*\*\* 页上向用户分配“仅供查看审核日志”或“审核日志”角色，则他们将无法搜索审核日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-139">If you assign a user the View-Only Audit Logs or Audit Logs role on the **Permissions** page in the Security & Compliance Center, they won't be able to search the audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-140">必须在 Exchange Online 中分配权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-140">You have to assign the permissions in Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-141">这是因为用于搜索审核日志的基础 cmdlet 是 Exchange Online cmdlet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-141">This is because the underlying cmdlet used to search the audit log is an Exchange Online cmdlet.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-142">当用户或管理员执行审核活动时，将生成审核记录并将其存储在组织的审核日志中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-142">When an audited activity is performed by a user or admin, an audit record is generated and stored in the audit log for your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-143">保留审核记录（并且可在审核日志中搜索）的时间长度取决于你的 Office 365 或 Microsoft 365 企业版订阅，具体而言是分配给特定用户的许可证类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-143">The length of time that an audit record is retained (and searchable in the audit log) depends on your Office 365 or Microsoft 365 Enterprise subscription, and specifically the type of the license that is assigned to specific users.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="85d61-144">对于分配了 Office 365 E5 或 Microsoft 365 E5 许可证的用户（或拥有 Microsoft 365 E5 合规版或 Microsoft 365 E5 电子数据展示和审核附加许可证的用户），Azure Active Directory、Exchange 和 SharePoint 活动的审核记录默认保留一年。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-144">For users assigned an Office 365 E5 or Microsoft 365 E5 license (or users with a Microsoft 365 E5 Compliance or Microsoft 365 E5 eDiscovery and Audit add-on license), audit records for Azure Active Directory, Exchange, and SharePoint activity are retained for one year by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-145">此外，组织还可以创建审核日志保留策略，以便将其他服务中的活动的审核记录保留最长一年时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-145">Organizations can also create audit log retention policies to retain audit records for activities in other services for up to one year.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-146">有关详细信息，请参阅[管理审核日志保留策略](audit-log-retention-policies.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-146">For more information, see [Manage audit log retention policies](audit-log-retention-policies.md).</span></span>

    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="85d61-147">如果组织参与了审计记录保留一年的个人预览版计划，则在正式发布日期之前产生的审核记录的保留期限不会被重置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-147">If your organization participated in the private preview program for the one-year retention of audit records, the retention duration for audit records that were generated before the general availability rollout date will not be reset.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="85d61-148">对于分配有任何其他（非E5）Office 365 或 Microsoft 365 许可证的用户，审核记录将保留90天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-148">For users assigned any other (non-E5) Office 365 or Microsoft 365 license, audit records are retained for 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-149">有关支持统一审核日志记录的 Office 365 和 Microsoft 365 订阅的列表，请参阅[安全与合规中心服务说明](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/servicedescriptions/office-365-platform-service-description/office-365-securitycompliance-center)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-149">For a list of Office 365 and Microsoft 365 subscriptions that support unified audit logging, see [the security and compliance center service description](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/servicedescriptions/office-365-platform-service-description/office-365-securitycompliance-center).</span></span>

    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="85d61-150">即使启用了默认启用的邮箱审核，也可能会发现无法在安全与合规中心的审核日志搜索中找到某些用户的邮箱审核事件，也无法通过 Office 365 管理活动 API 找到这些事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-150">Even when mailbox auditing on by default is turned on, you might notice that mailbox audit events for some users aren't found in audit log searches in the Security & Compliance Center or via the Office 365 Management Activity API.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-151">有关详细信息，请参阅[有关邮箱审核日志记录的详细信息](enable-mailbox-auditing.md#more-information)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-151">For more information, see [More information about mailbox audit logging](enable-mailbox-auditing.md#more-information).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-152">如果希望为组织关闭审核日志搜索，可以在连接到 Exchange Online 组织的远程 PowerShell 中运行以下命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-152">If you want to turn off audit log search for your organization, you can run the following command in remote PowerShell connected to your Exchange Online organization:</span></span>

  ```powershell
  Set-AdminAuditLogConfig -UnifiedAuditLogIngestionEnabled $false
  ```

    <span data-ttu-id="85d61-153">若要再次打开审核搜索，可在 Exchange Online PowerShell 中运行以下命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-153">To turn on audit search again, you can run the following command in Exchange Online PowerShell:</span></span>

  ```powershell
  Set-AdminAuditLogConfig -UnifiedAuditLogIngestionEnabled $true
  ```

  <span data-ttu-id="85d61-154">有关详细信息，请参阅[关闭审核日志搜索](turn-audit-log-search-on-or-off.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-154">For more information, see [Turn off audit log search](turn-audit-log-search-on-or-off.md).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-155">如前所述，用于搜索审核日志的基础 cmdlet 是 Exchange Online cmdlet，即 **Search-UnifiedAuditLog**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-155">As previously stated, the underlying cmdlet used to search the audit log is an Exchange Online cmdlet, which is **Search-UnifiedAuditLog**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-156">这意味着可使用此 cmdlet 搜索审核日志，而不是使用安全与合规中心中的“审核日志搜索”\*\*\*\* 页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-156">That means you can use this cmdlet to search the audit log instead of using the **Audit log search** page in the Security & Compliance Center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-157">必须在连接到 Exchange Online 组织的远程 PowerShell 中运行此 cmdlet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-157">You have to run this cmdlet in remote PowerShell connected to your Exchange Online organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-158">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Search-UnifiedAuditLog](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=834776)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-158">For more information, see [Search-UnifiedAuditLog](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=834776).</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="85d61-159">有关将 **Search-UnifiedAuditLog** cmdlet 所返回的搜索结果导出到 CSV 文件的信息，请参阅[导出、配置和查看审核日志记录](export-view-audit-log-records.md#tips-for-exporting-and-viewing-the-audit-log)中的“有关导出和查看审核日志的提示”部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-159">For information about exporting the search results returned by the **Search-UnifiedAuditLog** cmdlet to a CSV file, see the "Tips for exporting and viewing the audit log" section in [Export, configure, and view audit log records](export-view-audit-log-records.md#tips-for-exporting-and-viewing-the-audit-log).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-160">若想以编程方式从审核日志下载数据，建议使用 Office 365 管理活动 API，而不是使用 PowerShell 脚本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-160">If you want to programmatically download data from the audit log, we recommend that you use the Office 365 Management Activity API instead of using a PowerShell script.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-161">Office 365 管理活动 API 是一项 REST Web 服务，可用于为组织制定操作、安全和合规性监视解决方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-161">The Office 365 Management Activity API is a REST web service that you can use to develop operations, security, and compliance monitoring solutions for your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-162">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Office 365 管理活动 API 参考](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/office-365-management-api/office-365-management-activity-api-reference)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-162">For more information, see [Office 365 Management Activity API reference](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/office-365-management-api/office-365-management-activity-api-reference).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-163">发生事件后，最多需要 30 分钟到 24 小时即可在审核日志搜索的结果中返回相应的审核日志记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-163">It can take up to 30 minutes or up to 24 hours after an event occurs for the corresponding audit log record to be returned in the results of an audit log search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-164">下表显示了 Office 365 中不同服务所花费的时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-164">The following table shows the time it takes for the different services in Office 365.</span></span>

  |<span data-ttu-id="85d61-165">Microsoft 365 服务或功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-165">Microsoft 365 service or feature</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-166">30 分钟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-166">30 minutes</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-167">24 小时</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-167">24 hours</span></span>|
  |:-----|:-----:|:-----:|
  |<span data-ttu-id="85d61-168">高级威胁防护和威胁智能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-168">Advanced Threat Protection and Threat Intelligence</span></span>|![复选标记](../media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)||
  |<span data-ttu-id="85d61-170">Azure Active Directory（用户登录事件）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-170">Azure Active Directory (user login events)</span></span>||![复选标记](../media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)|
  |<span data-ttu-id="85d61-172">Azure Active Directory（管理员事件）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-172">Azure Active Directory (admin events)</span></span>||![复选标记](../media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)|
  |<span data-ttu-id="85d61-174">数据丢失防护</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-174">Data Loss Prevention</span></span>|![复选标记](../media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)||

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-208">Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) 是 Office 365 的目录服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-208">Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) is the directory service for Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-209">统一审核日志包含用户、组、应用程序、域以及在 Microsoft 365 管理中心或 Azure 管理门户中执行的目录活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-209">The unified audit log contains user, group, application, domain, and directory activities performed in the Microsoft 365 admin center or in the Azure management portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-210">有关 Azure AD 事件的完整列表，请参阅 [Azure Active Directory 审核报告事件](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=616549)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-210">For a complete list of Azure AD events, see [Azure Active Directory Audit Report Events](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=616549).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-211">默认情况下，Power BI 的审核日志记录未启用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-211">Audit logging for Power BI isn't enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-212">若要在审核日志中搜索 Power BI 活动，则必须在 Power BI 管理门户中启用审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-212">To search for Power BI activities in the audit log, you have to enable auditing in the Power BI admin portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-213">有关说明，请参阅 [Power BI 管理门户](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs)中的“审核日志”部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-213">For instructions, see the "Audit logs" section in [Power BI admin portal](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs).</span></span>

## <a name="search-the-audit-log"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-214">搜索审核日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-214">Search the audit log</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-215">下面介绍在 Office 365 中搜索审核日志的流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-215">Here's the process for searching the audit log in Office 365.</span></span>

[<span data-ttu-id="85d61-216">步骤 1：运行审核日志搜索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-216">Step 1: Run an audit log search</span></span>](#step-1-run-an-audit-log-search)

[<span data-ttu-id="85d61-217">步骤 2：查看搜索结果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-217">Step 2: View the search results</span></span>](#step-2-view-the-search-results)

[<span data-ttu-id="85d61-218">步骤 3：筛选搜索结果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-218">Step 3: Filter the search results</span></span>](#step-3-filter-the-search-results)

[<span data-ttu-id="85d61-219">步骤 4：将搜索结果导出到文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-219">Step 4: Export the search results to a file</span></span>](#step-4-export-the-search-results-to-a-file)

### <a name="step-1-run-an-audit-log-search"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-220">步骤 1：运行审核日志搜索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-220">Step 1: Run an audit log search</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="85d61-221">转到 [https://protection.office.com](https://protection.office.com)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-221">Go to [https://protection.office.com](https://protection.office.com).</span></span>

    > [!TIP]
    > <span data-ttu-id="85d61-222">使用专用浏览会话（而不是常规会话）来访问安全与合规中心，因为它会阻止你使用当前登录时使用的凭据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-222">Use a private browsing session (not a regular session) to access the Security & Compliance Center because this will prevent the credential that you are currently logged on with from being used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-223">若要在 Internet Explorer 或 Microsoft Edge 中打开 InPrivate 浏览会话，只需按 CTRL+SHIFT+P。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-223">To open an InPrivate Browsing session in Internet Explorer or Microsoft Edge, just press CTRL+SHIFT+P.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-224">若要在 Google Chrome（称为隐身窗口）中打开专用浏览会话，请按 CTRL+SHIFT+N。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-224">To open a private browsing session in Google Chrome (called an incognito window), press CTRL+SHIFT+N.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="85d61-225">使用工作或学校帐户进行登录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-225">Sign in using your work or school account.</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="85d61-226">在安全与合规中心的左侧窗格中，单击“**搜索**”，然后单击“**审核日志搜索**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-226">In the left pane of the Security & Compliance Center, click **Search**, and then click **Audit log search**.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="85d61-227">此时将显示“**审核日志搜索**”页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-227">The **Audit log search** page is displayed.</span></span>

    ![配置条件，然后单击“搜索”以运行报告](../media/8639d09c-2843-44e4-8b4b-9f45974ff7f1.png)

    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="85d61-229">必须首先打开审核日志记录，然后才能运行审核日志搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-229">You have to first turn on audit logging before you can run an audit log search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-230">如果显示“**开始记录用户和管理员活动**”链接，请单击该链接以打开审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-230">If the **Start recording user and admin activity** link is displayed, click it to turn on auditing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-231">如果未看到此链接，则已为你的组织开启审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-231">If you don't see this link, auditing has already been turned on for your organization.</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="85d61-232">配置以下搜索条件：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-232">Configure the following search criteria:</span></span>

   1. <span data-ttu-id="85d61-233">“**活动**”：单击下拉列表以显示你可以搜索的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-233">**Activities**: Click the drop-down list to display the activities that you can search for.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-234">已将用户和管理员活动整理到相关活动组中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-234">User and admin activities are organized into groups of related activities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-235">你可以选择特定活动，或单击活动组名称以选择该组中的所有活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-235">You can select specific activities or you can click the activity group name to select all activities in the group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-236">你也可以单击已选活动以取消选择。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-236">You can also click a selected activity to clear the selection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-237">运行搜索后，仅将显示所选活动的审核日志项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-237">After you run the search, only the audit log entries for the selected activities are displayed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-238">选择“**显示所有活动的结果**”将显示由所选用户或用户组执行的所有活动的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-238">Selecting **Show results for all activities** displays results for all activities performed by the selected user or group of users.</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="85d61-239">审核日志中记录了超过 100 个用户和管理员活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-239">Over 100 user and admin activities are logged in the audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-240">单击本文主题处的“已审核的活动”\*\*\*\* 选项卡可查看每个不同服务中每个活动的描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-240">Click the **Audited activities** tab at the topic of this article to see the descriptions of every activity in each of the different services.</span></span>

   1. <span data-ttu-id="85d61-241">“**开始日期**”和“**结束日期**”：默认选择了过去七天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-241">**Start date** and **End date**: The last seven days are selected by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-242">选择日期和时间范围，以显示在这段时间内发生的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-242">Select a date and time range to display the events that occurred within that period.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-243">日期和时间将以协调世界时 (UTC) 格式显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-243">The date and time are presented in Coordinated Universal Time (UTC) format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-244">可指定的最大日期范围为 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-244">The maximum date range that you can specify is 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-245">如果所选日期范围超过 90 天，将显示错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-245">An error is displayed if the selected date range is greater than 90 days.</span></span>

      > [!TIP]
      > <span data-ttu-id="85d61-246">如果要使用为期 90 天的最大日期范围，请选择当前时间作为“**开始日期**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-246">If you're using the maximum date range of 90 days, select the current time for the **Start date**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-247">否则，你将收到说明开始日期早于结束日期的错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-247">Otherwise, you'll receive an error saying that the start date is earlier than the end date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-248">如果你在过去 90 天内打开了审核，则最大日期范围不能从打开审核的日期之前开始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-248">If you've turned on auditing within the last 90 days, the maximum date range can't start before the date that auditing was turned on.</span></span>

   1. <span data-ttu-id="85d61-249">“**用户**”：单击此框，然后选择要为其显示搜索结果的一名或多名用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-249">**Users**: Click in this box and then select one or more users to display search results for.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-250">由你在此框中所选用户执行的所选活动的审核日志项目将显示在结果列表中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-250">The audit log entries for the selected activity performed by the users you select in this box are displayed in the list of results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-251">将此框留空以返回组织中所有用户（和服务帐户）的条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-251">Leave this box blank to return entries for all users (and service accounts) in your organization.</span></span>

   1. <span data-ttu-id="85d61-252">“**文件、文件夹或网站**”：键入部分或完整的文件或文件夹名称，搜索与包含指定关键字的文件夹文件相关的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-252">**File, folder, or site**: Type some or all of a file or folder name to search for activity related to the file of folder that contains the specified keyword.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-253">你还可以指定文件或文件夹的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-253">You can also specify a URL of a file or folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-254">如果使用 URL，请确保输入完整的 URL 路径，或者如果输入部分 URL，则请勿包含任何特殊字符或空格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-254">If you use a URL, be sure the type the full URL path or if you type a portion of the URL, don't include any special characters or spaces.</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="85d61-255">将此框留空以返回组织中所有文件和文件夹的条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-255">Leave this box blank to return entries for all files and folders in your organization.</span></span>

      > [!TIP]
      >
      > - <span data-ttu-id="85d61-256">如果要查找与**网站**相关的所有活动，请在 URL 后面添加通配符 (\*) 以返回该网站的所有条目，例如，**"https://contoso-my.sharepoint.com/personal/\*"**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-256">If you're looking for all activities related to a **site**, add the wildcard symbol (\*) after the URL to return all entries for that site; for example, **"https://contoso-my.sharepoint.com/personal/\*"**.</span></span>
      >
      > - <span data-ttu-id="85d61-257">如果要查找与**文件**相关的所有活动，请在文件名后面添加通配符 (\*) 以返回该文件的所有条目，例如，**"\*Customer_Profitability_Sample.csv"**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-257">If you're looking for all activities related to a **file**, add the wildcard symbol (\*) before the file name to return all entries for that file; for example, **"\*Customer_Profitability_Sample.csv"**.</span></span>

5. <span data-ttu-id="85d61-258">单击“**搜索**”以使用搜索条件运行搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-258">Click **Search** to run the search using your search criteria.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="85d61-259">此时将加载搜索结果，片刻后将显示在“**结果**”下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-259">The search results are loaded, and after a few moments they are displayed under **Results**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-260">完成搜索后会显示找到的结果数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-260">When the search is finished, the number of results found is displayed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-261">“**结果**”窗格中最多可显示 5,000 个事件（每次加载 150 个）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-261">A maximum of 5,000 events will be displayed in the **Results** pane in increments of 150 events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-262">如果超过 5,000 个事件满足搜索条件，则将显示最近的 5,000 个事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-262">If more than 5,000 events meet the search criteria, the most recent 5,000 events are displayed.</span></span>

   ![完成搜索后会显示结果数。](../media/986216f1-ca2f-4747-9480-e232b5bf094c.png)

#### <a name="tips-for-searching-the-audit-log"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-264">有关搜索审核日志的提示</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-264">Tips for searching the audit log</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-265">可以通过单击活动名称选择要搜索的特定活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-265">You can select specific activities to search for by clicking the activity name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-266">或者可以通过单击组名搜索该组中的所有活动（例如“**文件和文件夹活动**”）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-266">Or you can search for all activities in a group (such as **File and folder activities**) by clicking the group name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-267">如果选择了活动，可以单击该活动以取消选择。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-267">If an activity is selected, you can click it to cancel the selection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-268">还可以使用搜索框显示包含所键入关键字的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-268">You can also use the search box to display the activities that contain the keyword that you type.</span></span>

  ![单击活动组名称以选择所有活动](../media/3cde97cb-6f35-47c0-8612-ecd9c6ac36a3.png)

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-270">必须选择“**活动**”列表中的“**显示所有活动的结果**”才能显示 Exchange 管理员审核日志中的条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-270">You have to select **Show results for all activities** in the **Activities** list to display events from the Exchange admin audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-271">此审核日志中的事件将在结果的“**活动**”列中显示 cmdlet 名称（例如 **Set-Mailbox**）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-271">Events from this audit log display a cmdlet name (for example, **Set-Mailbox**) in the **Activity** column in the results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-272">有关详细信息，请单击本主题中的“**已审核的活动**”选项卡，然后单击“**Exchange 管理员活动**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-272">For more information, click the **Audited activities** tab in this topic and then click **Exchange admin activities**.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="85d61-273">同样，某些审核活动在“**活动**”列表中没有相应项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-273">Similarly, there are some auditing activities that don't have a corresponding item in the **Activities** list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-274">如果已知这些活动的操作名称，可搜索所有活动，然后通过在“**活动**”列对应的框中键入操作名称来筛选结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-274">If you know the name of the operation for these activities, you can search for all activities, then filter the results by typing the name of the operation in the box for the **Activity** column.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-275">有关筛选结果的详细信息，请参阅[步骤 3：筛选搜索结果](#step-3-filter-the-search-results)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-275">See [Step 3: Filter the search results](#step-3-filter-the-search-results) for more information about filtering the results.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-276">单击“**清除**”以清除当前搜索条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-276">Click **Clear** to clear the current search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-277">日期范围返回到默认值（过去七天）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-277">The date range returns to the default of the last seven days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-278">还可以单击“**全部清除以显示所有活动的结果**”以取消所有选定活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-278">You can also click **Clear all to show results for all activities** to cancel all selected activities.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-279">如果找到了 5,000 条结果，则可以假定可能存在超过 5,000 个符合搜索条件的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-279">If 5,000 results are found, you can probably assume that there are more than 5,000 events that met the search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-280">你可以优化搜索条件并重新运行搜索以返回较少结果，也可以通过选择“**导出结果**”\>“**下载所有结果**”导出所有搜索结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-280">You can either refine the search criteria and rerun the search to return fewer results, or you can export all of the search results by selecting **Export results** \> **Download all results**.</span></span>

### <a name="step-2-view-the-search-results"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-281">步骤 2：查看搜索结果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-281">Step 2: View the search results</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-282">审核日志搜索结果会显示在“**审核日志搜索**”页中的“**结果**”下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-282">The results of an audit log search are displayed under **Results** on the **Audit log search** page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-283">如上文所述，最多显示 5,000 个最新事件（每次加载 150 个）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-283">As previously stated a maximum of 5,000 (newest) events are displayed in increments of 150 events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-284">若要显示更多事件，可以使用“**结果**”窗格中的滚动条，或按 **Shift+End** 显示随后的 150 个事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-284">To display more events you can use the scroll bar in the **Results** pane or you can press **Shift + End** to display the next 150 events.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-285">结果包含有关搜索返回的每个事件的以下信息：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-285">The results contain the following information about each event returned by the search:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-286">“**日期**”：事件发生的日期和时间（采用 UTC 格式）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-286">**Date**: The date and time (in UTC format) when the event occurred.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-287">“**IP 地址**”：记录活动时所用设备的 IP 地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-287">**IP address**: The IP address of the device that was used when the activity was logged.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-288">IP 地址显示为 IPv4 或 IPv6 地址格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-288">The IP address is displayed in either an IPv4 or IPv6 address format.</span></span>

   > [!NOTE]
  > <span data-ttu-id="85d61-289">对于某些服务，此字段中显示的值可能是代表用户调用服务的受信任应用程序（例如，Web 应用上的 Office）的 IP 地址，而不是执行活动的人员所使用设备的 IP 地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-289">For some services, the value displayed in this field might be the IP address for a trusted application (for example, Office on the web apps) calling into the service on behalf of a user and not the IP address of the device used by person who performed the activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-290">此外，对于针对 Azure Active Directory 相关事件的管理员活动（或由系统帐户执行的活动），未记录 IP 地址，此字段中显示的值为 `null`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-290">Also, for admin activity (or activity performed by a system account) for Azure Active Directory-related events, the IP address isn't logged and the value displayed in this field is `null`.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-291">**用户**：执行触发事件的操作的用户（或服务帐户）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-291">**User**: The user (or service account) who performed the action that triggered the event.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-292">“**活动**”：用户执行的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-292">**Activity**: The activity performed by the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-293">此值对应于你在“**活动**”下拉列表中选定的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-293">This value corresponds to the activities that you selected in the **Activities** drop down list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-294">对于来自 Exchange 管理员审核日志的事件，此列中的值为 Exchange cmdlet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-294">For an event from the Exchange admin audit log, the value in this column is an Exchange cmdlet.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-295">“**项目**”：由于相应活动而创建或修改的对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-295">**Item**: The object that was created or modified as a result of the corresponding activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-296">例如已查看或修改的文件或已更新的用户帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-296">For example, the file that was viewed or modified or the user account that was updated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-297">并非所有活动在此列中都具有值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-297">Not all activities have a value in this column.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-298">“**详细信息**”：有关活动的其他详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-298">**Detail**: Additional information about an activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-299">同样，并非所有活动均具有值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-299">Again, not all activities have a value.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-300">单击“**结果**”下的列标题对结果进行排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-300">Click a column header under **Results** to sort the results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-301">你可以将结果按从 A 到 Z 或从 Z 到 A 的顺序排序。单击“**日期**”标题以将结果按从旧到新或从新到旧的顺序排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-301">You can sort the results from A to Z or Z to A. Click the **Date** header to sort the results from oldest to newest or newest to oldest.</span></span>

#### <a name="view-the-details-for-a-specific-event"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-302">查看特定事件的详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-302">View the details for a specific event</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-303">可以通过单击搜索结果列表中的事件记录查看有关事件的更多详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-303">You can view more details about an event by clicking the event record in the list of search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-304">此时将显示包含事件记录的详细属性的“**详细信息**”页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-304">A **Details** page is displayed that contains the detailed properties from the event record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-305">显示的属性取决于其中发生事件的服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-305">The properties that are displayed depend on the service in which the event occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-306">若要显示这些详细信息，请单击“**更多信息**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-306">To display these details, click **More information**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-307">有关说明，请参阅[审核日志中的属性详细信息](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-307">For descriptions, see [Detailed properties in the audit log](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md).</span></span>

![单击“详细信息”，查看审核日志事件记录的详细属性](../media/6df582ae-d339-4735-b1a6-80914fb77a08.png)

### <a name="step-3-filter-the-search-results"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-309">步骤 3：筛选搜索结果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-309">Step 3: Filter the search results</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-310">除排序外，你还可以筛选审核日志搜索的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-310">In addition to sorting, you can also filter the results of an audit log search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-311">这是一项可帮助你快速筛选特定用户或活动的结果的强大功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-311">This is a great feature that can help you quickly filter the results for a specific user or activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-312">你可以首先创建一个广泛的搜索范围，然后快速筛选结果以查看特定事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-312">You can initially create a wide search and then quickly filter the results to see specific events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-313">然后可以缩小搜索条件范围并重新运行搜索以返回更小、更简洁的结果集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-313">Then you can narrow the search criteria and rerun the search to return a smaller, more concise set of results.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-314">若要筛选结果，请执行以下操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-314">To filter the results:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="85d61-315">运行审核日志搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-315">Run an audit log search.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="85d61-316">结果显示后，单击“**筛选结果**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-316">When the results are displayed, click **Filter results**.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="85d61-317">每个列标题下将显示关键字框。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-317">Keyword boxes are displayed under each column header.</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="85d61-318">根据要筛选的列，单击列标题下的其中一个框并键入字词。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-318">Click one of the boxes under a column header and type a word or phrase, depending on the column you're filtering on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-319">结果将动态重新调整以显示符合筛选条件的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-319">The results will dynamically readjust to display the events that match your filter.</span></span>

   ![在筛选器中键入一个单词，以显示匹配筛选的事件](../media/542dc323-a997-402c-934b-cc5e218e50bc.png)

4. <span data-ttu-id="85d61-321">若要清除筛选器，请单击筛选器框中的“**X**”，或单击“**隐藏筛选**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-321">To clear a filter, click the **X** in the filter box or click **Hide filtering**.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-322">若要显示 Exchange 管理员审核日志中的事件，请在“**活动**”筛选器框中键入 **-**（破折号）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-322">To display events from the Exchange admin audit log, type a **-** (dash) in the **Activity** filter box.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-323">这将在 Exchange 管理员事件的“**活动**”列中显示 cmdlet 名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-323">This will display cmdlet names, which are displayed in the **Activity** column for Exchange admin events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-324">然后你便可按字母顺序对 cmdlet 名称进行排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-324">Then you can sort the cmdlet names in alphabetical order.</span></span>

### <a name="step-4-export-the-search-results-to-a-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-325">步骤 4：将搜索结果导出到文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-325">Step 4: Export the search results to a file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-326">可以将审核日志搜索的结果导出到本地计算机上的逗号分隔值 (CSV) 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-326">You can export the results of an audit log search to a comma-separated value (CSV) file on your local computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-327">可以在 Microsoft Excel 中打开此文件，然后使用搜索、排序、筛选和将（包含多个属性的）单列拆分为多列等功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-327">You can open this file in Microsoft Excel and use features such as search, sorting, filtering, and splitting a single column (that contains multiple properties) into multiple columns.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="85d61-328">运行审核日志搜索，然后修订搜索条件直到获得所需结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-328">Run an audit log search, and then revise the search criteria until you have the desired results.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="85d61-329">单击“**导出结果**”，然后选择下列选项之一：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-329">Click **Export results** and select one of the following options:</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="85d61-330">“**保存加载的结果**”：选择此选项可仅导出“**审核日志搜索**”页上“**结果**”之下显示的条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-330">**Save loaded results**: Choose this option to export only the entries that are displayed under **Results** on the **Audit log search** page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-331">下载的 CSV 文件包含（“日期”、“用户”、“活动”、“项目”和“详细信息”）页面上显示的相同列（和数据）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-331">The CSV file that is downloaded contains the same columns (and data) displayed on the page (Date, User, Activity, Item, and Details).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-332">包含审核日志项目中更多信息的 CSV 文件包括一额外列（名为“**更多**”）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-332">An extra column (named **More**) is included in the CSV file that contains more information from the audit log entry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-333">由于你将导出“**审核日志搜索**”页上已加载（且可查看）的相同结果，因此最多可导出 5,000 个条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-333">Because you're exporting the same results that are loaded (and viewable) on the **Audit log search** page, a maximum of 5,000 entries are exported.</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="85d61-334">“下载所有结果”\*\*\*\*：选择此选项可以导出符合搜索条件的审核日志中的所有条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-334">**Download all results**: Choose this option to export all entries from the audit log that meet the search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-335">对于较大的搜索结果集，选择此选项可下载审核日志的所有条目以及可在“**审核日志搜索**”页上显示的 5,000 条审核记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-335">For a large set of search results, choose this option to download all entries from the audit log in addition to the 5,000 audit records that can be displayed on the **Audit log search** page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-336">此选项会将原始数据从审核日志下载到 CSV 文件，并在名为“**AuditData**”的列中包含审核日志项目中的其他信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-336">This option downloads the raw data from the audit log to a CSV file, and contains additional information from the audit log entry in a column named **AuditData**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-337">如果选择此导出选项，下载该文件可能需要更长时间，因为文件可能比选择其他选项下载的文件大得多。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-337">It may take longer to download the file if you choose this export option because the file may be much larger than the one that's downloaded if you choose the other option.</span></span>

     > [!IMPORTANT]
     > <span data-ttu-id="85d61-338">你可以将最多 50,000 个条目从单个审核日志搜索中下载到 CSV 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-338">You can download a maximum of 50,000 entries to a CSV file from a single audit log search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-339">如果下载了 50,000 个条目到 CSV 文件，则可以假定可能存在超过 50,000 个符合搜索条件的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-339">If 50,000 entries are downloaded to the CSV file, you can probably assume there are more than 50,000 events that met the search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-340">若要导出的条目超出此限制，请尝试使用日期范围以减少审核日志项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-340">To export more than this limit, try using a date range to reduce the number of audit log entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-341">你可能需要使用更小日期范围运行多个搜索来导出超过 50,000 个条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-341">You might have to run multiple searches with smaller date ranges to export more than 50,000 entries.</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="85d61-342">选择导出选项后，窗口底部将显示一条消息，提示你打开 CSV 文件并将其保存到“下载”文件夹或特定文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-342">After you select an export option, a message is displayed at the bottom of the window that prompts you to open the CSV file, save it to the Downloads folder, or save it to a specific folder.</span></span>

#### <a name="more-information-about-exporting-and-viewing-audit-log-search-results"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-343">有关导出和查看审核日志搜索结果的详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-343">More information about exporting and viewing audit log search results</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-344">如果下载所有搜索结果，则 CSV 文件将包含一个名为“**AuditData**”的列，其中包含每个事件的其他信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-344">If you download all search results, the CSV file contains a column named **AuditData**, which contains additional information about each event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-345">此列中的数据由一个 JSON 对象组成，其中包含审核日志记录中的多个属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-345">The data in this column consists of a JSON object that contains multiple properties from the audit log record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-346">JSON 对象中的每个 *property:value* 对均由逗号分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-346">Each *property:value* pair in the JSON object is separated by a comma.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-347">你可以使用 Excel 中的 Power Query 编辑器的 JSON 转换工具将“**AuditData**”列拆分为多个列，以使 JSON 对象中的每个属性具有自己的列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-347">You can use the JSON transform tool in the Power Query Editor in Excel to split **AuditData** column into multiple columns so that each property in the JSON object has its own column.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-348">这让你能够对一个或多个属性进行排序和筛选。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-348">This lets you sort and filter on one or more of these properties.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-349">有关使用 Power Query 编辑器转换 JSON 对象的分步说明，请参阅[导出、配置和查看审核日志记录](export-view-audit-log-records.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-349">For step-by-step instructions using the Power Query Editor to transform the JSON object, see [Export, configure, and view audit log records](export-view-audit-log-records.md).</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="85d61-350">拆分“**AuditData**”列后，你可以对“**操作**”列进行筛选以显示特定类型活动的详细属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-350">After you split the **AuditData** column, you can filter on the **Operations** column to display the detailed properties for a specific type of activity.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-351">“下载所有结果”\*\*\*\* 选项可将原始数据从审核日志下载到 CSV 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-351">The **Download all results** option downloads the raw data from the audit log to a CSV file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-352">此文件包含的列名（“CreationDate”、“UserIds”、“操作”、“AuditData”）与选择“**保存已加载结果**”选项时下载的文件列名不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-352">This file contains different column names (CreationDate, UserIds, Operation, AuditData) than the file that's downloaded if you select the **Save loaded results** option.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-353">对于同一活动，两个不同 CSV 文件中的值可能也有所不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-353">The values in the two different CSV files for the same activity may also be different.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-354">例如，CSV 文件的“**操作**”列中的活动值可能与显示在“**审核日志搜索**”页上的“**活动**”列中的“用户友好”名称不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-354">For example, the activity in the **Action** column in the CSV file and may have a different value than the "user-friendly" name that's displayed in the **Activity** column on the **Audit log search** page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-355">例如，分别为“MailboxLogin”与“用户已登录到邮箱”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-355">For example, MailboxLogin vs. User signed in to mailbox.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-356">下载（包含来自不同服务的事件的）搜索查询的所有结果时，CSV 文件中的“AuditData”\*\*\*\* 列将含有不同属性，具体取决于在哪种服务中执行操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-356">When you download all results from a search query that contains events from different services, the **AuditData** column in the CSV file contains different properties depending on which service the action was performed in.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-357">例如，来自 Exchange 和 Azure AD 审核日志的条目包含一个名为 **ResultStatus** 的属性，它指示操作是否成功。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-357">For example, entries from Exchange and Azure AD audit logs include a property named **ResultStatus** that indicates if the action was successful or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-358">来自 SharePoint 的事件不包含此属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-358">This property isn't included for events in SharePoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-359">类似地，SharePoint 事件具有用于标识文件和文件夹相关活动的网站 URL 的属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-359">Similarly, SharePoint events have a property that identifies the site URL for file and folder-related activities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-360">若要缓和此行为，建议使用多个搜索导出单个服务中活动的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-360">To mitigate this behavior, consider using different searches to export the results for activities from a single service.</span></span>

  <span data-ttu-id="85d61-361">有关下载所有结果时 CSV 文件的“**AuditData**”列中所列各个属性的说明以及每个属性适用的服务，请参阅[审核日志中的属性详细信息](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-361">For a description of many of the properties that are listed in the **AuditData** column in the CSV file when you download all results, and the service each one applies to, see [Detailed properties in the audit log](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md).</span></span>

## <a name="audited-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-362">已审核的活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-362">Audited activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-363">本节中的表介绍了 Office 365 中经审核的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-363">The tables in this section describe the activities that are audited in Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-364">你可以通过在安全与合规中心中搜索审核日志来搜索这些事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-364">You can search for these events by searching the audit log in the security and compliance center.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-365">这些表对相关活动或特定服务中的活动进行分组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-365">These tables group related activities or the activities from a specific service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-366">表中包含显示在“**活动**”下拉列表中的友好名称以及导出搜索结果时显示在审核记录详细信息和 CSV 文件中的相应操作的名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-366">The tables include the friendly name that's displayed in the **Activities** drop-down list and the name of the corresponding operation that appears in the detailed information of an audit record and in the CSV file when you export the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-367">有关详细信息的说明，请参阅[审核日志中的属性详细信息](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-367">For descriptions of the detailed information, see [Detailed properties in the audit log](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md).</span></span>

### <a name="file-and-page-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-400">文件和页面活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-400">File and page activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-401">下表介绍了 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的文件和页面活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-401">The following table describes the file and page activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-402">友好名称</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-402">Friendly name</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-403">操作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-403">Operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-404">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-404">Description</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-405">已访问文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-405">Accessed file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-406">FileAccessed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-406">FileAccessed</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-407">用户或系统帐户访问文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-407">User or system account accesses a file.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-408">(无)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-408">(none)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-409">FileAccessedExtended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-409">FileAccessedExtended</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-410">这与“已访问文件”(FileAccessed) 活动有关。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-410">This is related to the "Accessed file" (FileAccessed) activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-411">如果一个用户长时间（至 3 小时）持续访问某一文件，则会记录下 FileAccessedExtended 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-411">A FileAccessedExtended event is logged when the same person continually accesses a file for an extended period (up to 3 hours).</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-412">记录 FileAccessedExtended 事件是为了减少持续访问文件时所记录的 FileAccessed 事件数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-412">The purpose of logging FileAccessedExtended events is to reduce the number of FileAccessed events that are logged when a file is continually accessed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-413">这有助于减小（实际上是）同一用户活动的多个 FileAccessed 记录的干扰，从而专注于初始（和更重要的）FileAccessed 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-413">This helps reduce the noise of multiple FileAccessed records for what is essentially the same user activity, and lets you focus on the initial (and more important) FileAccessed event.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-414">已更改文件的保留标签</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-414">Changed retention label for a file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-415">ComplianceSettingChanged</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-415">ComplianceSettingChanged</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-416">保留标签已应用于文档或已从文档中删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-416">A retention label was applied to or removed from a document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-417">手动或自动将保留标签应用于消息时触发此事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-417">This event is triggered when a retention label is manually or automatically applied to a message.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-418">已将记录状态更改为“已锁定”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-418">Changed record status to locked</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-419">LockRecord</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-419">LockRecord</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-420">将文档分类为记录的保留标签的记录状态为“已锁定”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-420">The record status of a retention label that classifies a document as a record was locked.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-421">这意味着无法修改或删除文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-421">This means the document can't be modified or deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-422">仅至少分配有网站参与者权限的用户才能更改文档的记录状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-422">Only users assigned at least the contributor permission for a site can change the record status of a document.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-423">已将记录状态更改为“未锁定”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-423">Changed record status to unlocked</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-424">UnlockRecord</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-424">UnlockRecord</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-425">将文档分类为记录的保留标签的记录状态为“未锁定”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-425">The record status of a retention label that classifies a document as a record was unlocked.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-426">这意味着可以修改或删除文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-426">This means that the document can be modified or deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-427">仅至少分配有网站参与者权限的用户才能更改文档的记录状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-427">Only users assigned at least the contributor permission for a site can change the record status of a document.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-428">已签入文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-428">Checked in file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-429">FileCheckedIn</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-429">FileCheckedIn</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-430">用户签入其从文档库中签出的文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-430">User checks in a document that they checked out from a document library.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-452">检测到文档敏感度不匹配</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-452">Detected document sensitivity mismatch</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-453">DocumentSensitivityMismatchDetected</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-453">DocumentSensitivityMismatchDetected</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-454">用户将文档上传到受敏感度标签保护的网站上，该文档的敏感度标签的优先级比该网站应用的敏感度标签高。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-454">User uploads a document to a site that's protected with a sensitivity label and the document has a higher priority sensitivity label than the sensitivity label applied to the site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-455">例如，标有“机密”的文档上传到标有“常规”的网站上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-455">For example, a document labeled Confidential is uploaded to a site labeled General.</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-456">如果文档的敏感度标签的优先级低于网站应用的敏感度标签，则不触发此事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-456">This event isn't triggered if the document has a lower priority sensitivity label than the sensitivity label applied to the site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-457">例如，标有“常规”的文档上传到标有“机密”的网站上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-457">For example, a document labeled General is uploaded to a site labeled Confidential.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-458">有关敏感度标签优先级的详细信息，请参阅[标签优先级（顺序）](sensitivity-labels.md#label-priority-order-matters)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-458">For more information about sensitivity label priority, see [Label priority (order matters)](sensitivity-labels.md#label-priority-order-matters).</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-472">(无)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-472">(none)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-473">FileModifiedExtended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-473">FileModifiedExtended</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-474">这与“已修改文件”(FileModified) 活动相关。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-474">This is related to the "Modified file" (FileModified) activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-475">如果一个用户长时间（至 3 小时）持续修改某一文件，则会记录下 FileModifiedExtended 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-475">A FileModifiedExtended event is logged when the same person continually modifies a file for an extended period (up to 3 hours).</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-476">记录 FileModifiedExtended 事件是为了减少持续修改文件时所记录的 FileModified 事件数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-476">The purpose of logging FileModifiedExtended events is to reduce the number of FileModified events that are logged when a file is continually modified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-477">这有助于减小（实际上是）同一用户活动的多个 FileModified 记录的干扰，从而专注于初始（和更重要的）FileModified 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-477">This helps reduce the noise of multiple FileModified records for what is essentially the same user activity, and lets you focus on the initial (and more important) FileModified event.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-514">(无)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-514">(none)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-515">PageViewedExtended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-515">PageViewedExtended</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-516">这与“已查看页面”(PageViewed) 活动相关。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-516">This is related to the "Viewed page" (PageViewed) activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-517">如果一个用户长时间（至 3 小时）持续查看某一网页，则会记录下 PageViewedExtended 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-517">A PageViewedExtended event is logged when the same person continually views a web page for an extended period (up to 3 hours).</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-518">记录 PageViewedExtended 事件是为了减少持续查看页面时所记录的 PageViewed 事件数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-518">The purpose of logging PageViewedExtended events is to reduce the number of PageViewed events that are logged when a page is continually viewed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-519">这有助于减小（实际上是）同一用户活动的多个 PageViewed 记录的干扰，从而专注于初始（和更重要的）PageViewed 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-519">This helps reduce the noise of multiple PageViewed records for what is essentially the same user activity, and lets you focus on the initial (and more important) PageViewed event.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-520">按客户端查看信号</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-520">View signaled by client</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-521">ClientViewSignaled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-521">ClientViewSignaled</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-522">用户的客户端（例如网站或移动应用）已发出信号，表明用户已查看指示的页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-522">A user's client (such as website or mobile app) has signaled that the indicated page has been viewed by the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-523">此活动通常在页面的 PagePrefetched 事件后记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-523">This activity is often logged following a PagePrefetched event for a page.</span></span> <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="85d61-524">**注意**：由于 ClientViewSignaled 事件由客户端而非服务器发出信号，因此服务器可能不会记录该事件，从而导致该事件可能未显示在审核日志中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-524">**NOTE**: Because ClientViewSignaled events are signaled by the client, rather than the server, it's possible the event may not be logged by the server and therefore may not appear in the audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-525">审核记录中的信息也可能不可信。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-525">It's also possible that information in the audit record may not be trustworthy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-526">但是，由于用户身份由用于创建信号的令牌验证，因此相应审核记录中列出的用户身份是准确的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-526">However, because the user's identity is validated by the token used to create the signal, the user's identity listed in the corresponding audit record is accurate.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-527">(无)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-527">(none)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-528">PagePrefetched</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-528">PagePrefetched</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-529">用户的客户端（例如网站或移动应用）已请求指示的页面，以帮助提高用户浏览时的性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-529">A user's client (such as website or mobile app) has requested the indicated page to help improve performance if the user browses to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-530">记录此事件以指示页面内容已服务于用户的客户端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-530">This event is logged to indicate that the page content has been served to the user's client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-531">此事件未明确指示用户导航到页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-531">This event isn't a definitive indication that the user navigated to the page.</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-532">当客户端（根据用户请求）呈现页面内容时，应生成 ClientViewSignaled 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-532">When the page content is rendered by the client (as per the user's request) a ClientViewSignaled event should be generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-533">并非所有客户端都支持指示预提取，因此一些预提取的活动可能会被记录为 PageViewed 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-533">Not all clients support indicating a pre-fetch, and therefore some pre-fetched activities might instead be logged as PageViewed events.</span></span>|
||||

#### <a name="the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-534">审核记录中的 app\@sharepoint 用户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-534">The app\@sharepoint user in audit records</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-535">在某些文件活动（和其他 SharePoint 相关活动）的审核记录中，你可能会注意到执行该活动的用户（在“用户”和“用户 ID”字段中识别）是 app@sharepoint。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-535">In audit records for some file activities (and other SharePoint-related activities), you may notice the user who performed the activity (identified in the User and UserId fields) is app@sharepoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-536">这表示执行活动的“用户”是一个应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-536">This indicates that the "user" who performed the activity was an application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-537">在这种情况下，该应用程序被授予 SharePoint 中代表用户、管理员或服务执行组织范围内操作（例如，搜索 SharePoint 网站或 OneDrive 帐户）的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-537">In this case, the application was granted permissions in SharePoint to perform organization-wide actions (such as search a SharePoint site or OneDrive account) on behalf of a user, admin, or service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-538">授予应用程序权限的过程被称为“*仅限 SharePoint 应用*”访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-538">This process of giving permissions to an application is called *SharePoint App-Only* access.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-539">这表明提供给 SharePoint 执行操作的身份验证是由应用程序而不是用户做出的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-539">This indicates that the authentication presented to SharePoint to perform an action was made by an application, instead of a user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-540">这就是为什么在某些审核记录中标识 app@sharepoint 用户的原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-540">This is why the app@sharepoint user is identified in certain audit records.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-541">有关详细信息，请参阅[通过仅限 SharePoint 应用授予访问权限](https://docs.microsoft.com/sharepoint/dev/solution-guidance/security-apponly-azureacs)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-541">For more information, see [Grant access using SharePoint App-Only](https://docs.microsoft.com/sharepoint/dev/solution-guidance/security-apponly-azureacs).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-542">例如，app@sharepoint 通常被标识为“已执行搜索查询”和“已访问文件”事件的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-542">For example, app@sharepoint is often identified as the user for "Performed search query" and "Accessed file" events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-543">这是因为在将保留策略应用到网站和 OneDrive 帐户时，组织中具有仅限 SharePoint 应用访问权限的应用程序会执行搜索查询和访问文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-543">That's because an application with SharePoint App-Only access in your organization performs search queries and accesses files when applying retention policies to sites and OneDrive accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-544">以下是一些其他情形，其中审核记录中的 app@sharepoint 可能被标识为执行活动的用户：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-544">Here are a few other scenarios where app@sharepoint may be identified in an audit record as the user who performed an activity:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-545">Microsoft 365 组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-545">Microsoft 365 Groups.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-546">用户或管理员创建新组时，会生成审核记录，用于创建网站集、更新列表以及将成员添加到 SharePoint 组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-546">When a user or admin creates a new group, audit records are generated for creating a site collection, updating lists, and adding members to a SharePoint group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-547">应用程序将代表创建组的用户执行这些任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-547">These tasks are performed an application on behalf of the user who created the group.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-548">Microsoft Teams。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-548">Microsoft Teams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-549">与 Microsoft 365 组类似，也会生成审核记录，用于创建网站集、更新列表以及在创建团队时将成员添加到 SharePoint 组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-549">Similar to Microsoft 365 Groups, audit records are generated for creating a site collection, updating lists, and adding members to a SharePoint group when a team is created.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-550">合规性功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-550">Compliance features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-551">管理员实现合规性功能（如保留策略、电子数据展示保留和自动应用敏感度标签）时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-551">When an admin implements compliance features, such as retention policies, eDiscovery holds, and auto-applying sensitivity labels.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-552">在这些和其他情形下，你还会注意到，以 app@sharepoint 作为指定用户的多个审核记录是在较短的时间范围内创建的，通常每条记录只需几秒钟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-552">In these and other scenarios, you'll also notice that multiple audit records with app@sharepoint as the specified user were created within a short time frame, often within a few seconds of each other.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-553">这也表明它们可能由同一个用户启动的任务触发。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-553">This also indicates they were probably triggered by the same user-initiated task.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-554">而且，审核记录中的 ApplicationDisplayName 和 EventData 字段可以帮助你识别触发此事件的应用场景或应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-554">Also, the ApplicationDisplayName and EventData fields in the audit record may help you identify the scenario or application that triggered the event.</span></span>

### <a name="folder-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-555">文件夹活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-555">Folder activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-556">下表介绍了 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的文件夹活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-556">The following table describes the folder activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-557">如前所述，某些 SharePoint 活动的审核记录将表明 app@sharepoint 用户代表启动操作的用户或管理员执行了该活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-557">As previously explained, audit records for some SharePoint activities will indicate the app@sharepoint user performed the activity of behalf of the user or admin who initiated the action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-558">有关详细信息，请参阅[审核记录中的 app\@sharepoint 用户](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-558">For more information, see [The app\@sharepoint user in audit records](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records).</span></span>
