### <a name="sharepoint-list-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-590">SharePoint 列表活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-590">SharePoint list activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-591">下表介绍了当用户与 SharePoint Online 中的列表和列表项进行交互时执行的相关活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-591">The following table describes activities related to when users interact with lists and list items in SharePoint Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-592">如前所述，某些 SharePoint 活动的审核记录将表明 app@sharepoint 用户代表启动操作的用户或管理员执行了该活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-592">As previously explained, audit records for some SharePoint activities will indicate the app@sharepoint user performed the activity of behalf of the user or admin who initiated the action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-593">有关详细信息，请参阅[审核记录中的 app\@sharepoint 用户](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-593">For more information, see [The app\@sharepoint user in audit records](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-594">友好名称</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-594">Friendly name</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-595">操作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-595">Operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-596">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-596">Description</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-597">已创建列表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-597">Created list</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-598">ListCreated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-598">ListCreated</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-599">用户已创建 SharePoint 列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-599">A user created a SharePoint list.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-600">已创建列表列</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-600">Created list column</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-601">ListColumnCreated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-601">ListColumnCreated</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-602">用户已创建 SharePoint 列表列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-602">A user created a SharePoint list column.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-603">列表列是指附加到一个或多个 SharePoint 列表的列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-603">A list column is a column that's attached to one or more SharePoint lists.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-604">已创建列表内容类型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-604">Created list content type</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-605">ListContentTypeCreated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-605">ListContentTypeCreated</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-606">用户已创建列表内容类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-606">A user created a list content type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-607">列表内容类型是指附加到一个或多个 SharePoint 列表的内容类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-607">A list content type is a content type that's attached to one or more SharePoint lists.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-608">已创建列表项</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-608">Created list item</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-609">ListItemCreated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-609">ListItemCreated</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-610">用户已在现有的 SharePoint 列表中创建项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-610">A user created an item in an existing SharePoint list.</span></span>|

### <a name="sharing-and-access-request-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-665">共享和访问请求活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-665">Sharing and access request activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-666">下表介绍了 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的用户共享和访问请求活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-666">The following table describes the user sharing and access request activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-667">对于共享事件，“**结果**”下的“**详细信息**”列标识了与之共享项目的用户名或组名以及该用户或组是否为组织中的成员或来宾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-667">For sharing events, the **Detail** column under **Results** identifies the name of the user or group the item was shared with and whether that user or group is a member or guest in your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-668">有关详细信息，请参阅[在审核日志中使用共享审核](use-sharing-auditing.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-668">For more information, see [Use sharing auditing in the audit log](use-sharing-auditing.md).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-669">根据用户对象的 UserType 属性，用户可以是*成员*或*来宾*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-669">Users can be either  *members*  or  *guests*  based on the UserType property of the user object.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-670">通常，成员为员工，来宾则为组织外部的合作者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-670">A member is usually an employee, and a guest is usually a collaborator outside of your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-671">用户接受共享邀请（而尚未成为你组织的一员）时，将在组织的目录中为其创建来宾帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-671">When a user accepts a sharing invitation (and isn't already part of your organization), a guest account is created for them in your organization's directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-672">来宾用户在你的目录中拥有帐户后，即可与其直接共享资源（无需邀请）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-672">Once the guest user has an account in your directory, resources may be shared directly with them (without requiring an invitation).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-673">友好名称</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-673">Friendly name</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-674">操作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-674">Operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-675">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-675">Description</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-679">已接受访问请求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-679">Accepted access request</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-680">AccessRequestAccepted</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-680">AccessRequestAccepted</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-681">已接受对网站、文件夹或文档的访问请求，并已授予请求用户访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-681">An access request to a site, folder, or document was accepted and the requesting user has been granted access.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-682">已接受共享邀请</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-682">Accepted sharing invitation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-683">SharingInvitationAccepted</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-683">SharingInvitationAccepted</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-684">用户（成员或来宾）接受共享邀请并被授予对资源的访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-684">User (member or guest) accepted a sharing invitation and was granted access to a resource.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-685">此事件包含受邀用户的信息以及用于接受邀请的电子邮件地址（可能有所不同）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-685">This event includes information about the user who was invited and the email address that was used to accept the invitation (they could be different).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-686">此活动通常伴有第二事件，描述向用户授予资源访问权限的方式，例如将用户添加到可以访问资源的组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-686">This activity is often accompanied by a second event that describes how the user was granted access to the resource, for example, adding the user to a group that has access to the resource.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-687">已阻止共享邀请</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-687">Blocked sharing invitation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-688">SharingInvitationBlocked</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-688">SharingInvitationBlocked</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-689">由于基于目标用户的域允许或拒绝外部共享的外部共享策略，已阻止组织中的用户发送的共享邀请。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-689">A sharing invitation sent by a user in your organization is blocked because of an external sharing policy that either allows or denies external sharing based on the domain of the target user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-690">在这种情况下，阻止共享邀请的原因如下：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-690">In this case, the sharing invitation was blocked because:</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-691">允许的域列表中不包含目标用户的域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-691">The target user's domain isn't included in the list of allowed domains.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-692">或</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-692">Or</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-693">目标用户的域包含在阻止的域列表中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-693">The target user's domain is included in the list of blocked domains.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-694">有关基于域允许或阻止外部共享的详细信息，请参阅 [SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的受限域共享](https://docs.microsoft.com/sharepoint/restricted-domains-sharing)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-694">For more information about allowing or blocking external sharing based on domains, see [Restricted domains sharing in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business](https://docs.microsoft.com/sharepoint/restricted-domains-sharing).</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-695">已创建访问请求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-695">Created access request</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-696">AccessRequestCreated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-696">AccessRequestCreated</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-697">用户请求访问其无权访问的网站、文件夹或文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-697">User requests access to a site, folder, or document they don't have permissions to access.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-703">已创建匿名链接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-703">Created an anonymous link</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-704">AnonymousLinkCreated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-704">AnonymousLinkCreated</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-705">用户创建了指向某资源的匿名链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-705">User created an anonymous link to a resource.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-706">拥有此链接的任何人均可访问资源，无需通过身份验证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-706">Anyone with this link can access the resource without having to be authenticated.</span></span>|

### <a name="synchronization-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-765">同步活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-765">Synchronization activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-766">下表列出了 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的文件同步活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-766">The following table lists file synchronization activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-767">友好名称</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-767">Friendly name</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-768">操作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-768">Operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-769">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-769">Description</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-770">已允许计算机同步文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-770">Allowed computer to sync files</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-771">ManagedSyncClientAllowed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-771">ManagedSyncClientAllowed</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-772">用户成功建立与网站的同步关系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-772">User successfully establishes a sync relationship with a site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-773">同步关系之所以成功，是因为用户计算机是添加到域列表（称为*安全收件人列表*）的域成员，可以访问组织中的文档库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-773">The sync relationship is successful because the user's computer is a member of a domain that's been added to the list of domains (called the *safe recipients list*) that can access document libraries in your organization.</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-774">有关此功能的详细信息，请参阅[使用 Windows PowerShell cmdlet 为安全收件人列表中的域启用 OneDrive 同步](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-774">For more information about this feature, see [Use Windows PowerShell cmdlets to enable OneDrive sync for domains that are on the safe recipients list](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609).</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-775">已阻止计算机同步文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-775">Blocked computer from syncing files</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-776">UnmanagedSyncClientBlocked</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-776">UnmanagedSyncClientBlocked</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-777">用户尝试从某计算机与网站建立同步关系，该计算机不是组织域的成员，或是尚未添加到可访问组织文档库的域列表（称为*安全收件人列表*）的域的成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-777">User tries to establish a sync relationship with a site from a computer that isn't a member of your organization's domain or is a member of a domain that hasn't been added to the list of domains (called the  *safe recipients list)*  that can access document libraries in your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-778">不允许同步关系，并阻止用户计算机在文档库上同步、下载或上传文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-778">The sync relationship is not allowed, and the user's computer is blocked from syncing, downloading, or uploading files on a document library.</span></span> <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-779">有关此功能的信息，请参阅[使用 Windows PowerShell cmdlet 为安全收件人列表中的域启用 OneDrive 同步](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-779">For information about this feature, see [Use Windows PowerShell cmdlets to enable OneDrive sync for domains that are on the safe recipients list](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609).</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-780">已将文件下载到计算机</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-780">Downloaded files to computer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-781">FileSyncDownloadedFull</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-781">FileSyncDownloadedFull</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-782">用户建立同步关系，并首次成功将文件从文档库下载到计算机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-782">User establishes a sync relationship and successfully downloads files for the first time to their computer from a document library.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-783">已将文件更改下载到计算机</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-783">Downloaded file changes to computer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-784">FileSyncDownloadedPartial</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-784">FileSyncDownloadedPartial</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-785">用户从文档库成功下载对文件所做的任何更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-785">User successfully downloads any changes to files from a document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-786">此活动表明对文档库中的文件所做的任何更改均已被下载到用户计算机中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-786">This activity indicates that any changes that were made to files in the document library were downloaded to the user's computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-787">仅下载了更改，因为用户以前下载过文档库（如**已将文件下载到计算机**活动所示）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-787">Only changes were downloaded because the document library was previously downloaded by the user (as indicated by the **Downloaded files to computer** activity).</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-788">已将文件上传到文档库</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-788">Uploaded files to document library</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-789">FileSyncUploadedFull</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-789">FileSyncUploadedFull</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-790">用户建立同步关系，并首次成功将文件从计算机上传到文档库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-790">User establishes a sync relationship and successfully uploads files for the first time from their computer to a document library.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-791">已将文件更改上传到文档库</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-791">Uploaded file changes to document library</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-792">FileSyncUploadedPartial</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-792">FileSyncUploadedPartial</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-793">用户成功上传对文档库中的文件所做的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-793">User successfully uploads changes to files on a document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-794">此事件表明对文档库文件的本地版本所做的任何更改都已成功上传到文档库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-794">This event indicates that any changes made to the local version of a file from a document library are successfully uploaded to the document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-795">仅已上传更改内容，因为用户以前上传过这些文件（如**已将文件上传到文档库**活动所示）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-795">Only changes are uploaded because those files were previously uploaded by the user (as indicated by the **Uploaded files to document library** activity).</span></span>|
||||

### <a name="site-permissions-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-796">网站权限活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-796">Site permissions activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-797">下表列出了与在 SharePoint 中分配权限以及使用组授予（和撤销）网站访问权限相关的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-797">The following table lists events related to assigning permissions in SharePoint and using groups to give (and revoke) access to sites.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-798">如前所述，某些 SharePoint 活动的审核记录将表明 app@sharepoint 用户代表启动操作的用户或管理员执行了该活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-798">As previously explained, audit records for some SharePoint activities will indicate the app@sharepoint user performed the activity of behalf of the user or admin who initiated the action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-799">有关详细信息，请参阅[审核记录中的 app\@sharepoint 用户](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-799">For more information, see [The app\@sharepoint user in audit records](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-800">友好名称</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-800">Friendly name</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-801">操作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-801">Operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-802">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-802">Description</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-803">已添加网站集管理员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-803">Added site collection admin</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-804">SiteCollectionAdminAdded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-804">SiteCollectionAdminAdded</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-805">网站集管理员或所有者为网站添加了作为网站集管理员的人员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-805">Site collection administrator or owner adds a person as a site collection administrator for a site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-806">网站集管理员具有网站集和所有子网站的完全控制权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-806">Site collection administrators have full control permissions for the site collection and all subsites.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-807">当管理员（通过编辑 SharePoint 管理中心的用户配置文件或[使用 Microsoft 365 管理中心](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/admin/add-users/get-access-to-and-back-up-a-former-user-s-data)）向自己授予对用户 OneDrive 帐户的访问权限时，也将记录此活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-807">This activity is also logged when an admin gives themselves access to a user's OneDrive account (by editing the user profile in the SharePoint admin center or by [using the Microsoft 365 admin center](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/admin/add-users/get-access-to-and-back-up-a-former-user-s-data)).</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-808">已向 SharePoint 组添加用户或组</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-808">Added user or group to SharePoint group</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-809">AddedToGroup</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-809">AddedToGroup</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-810">用户向 SharePoint 组添加了成员或来宾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-810">User added a member or guest to a SharePoint group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-811">这可能是目的性操作，也可能是其他活动（例如共享事件）的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-811">This might have been an intentional action or the result of another activity, such as a sharing event.</span></span>|

### <a name="site-administration-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-864">网站管理活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-864">Site administration activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-865">下表列出了 SharePoint Online 中的网站管理任务所产生的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-865">The following table lists events that result from site administration tasks in SharePoint Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-866">如前所述，某些 SharePoint 活动的审核记录将表明 app@sharepoint 用户代表启动操作的用户或管理员执行了该活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-866">As previously explained, audit records for some SharePoint activities will indicate the app@sharepoint user performed the activity of behalf of the user or admin who initiated the action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-867">有关详细信息，请参阅[审核记录中的 app\@sharepoint 用户](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-867">For more information, see [The app\@sharepoint user in audit records](#the-appsharepoint-user-in-audit-records).</span></span>

### <a name="exchange-mailbox-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-985">Exchange 邮箱活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-985">Exchange mailbox activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-986">下表列出了可以由邮箱审核日志记录的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-986">The following table lists the activities that can be logged by mailbox audit logging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-987">在审核日志中自动将由邮箱所有者、委派用户或管理员执行的邮箱活动记录长达 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-987">Mailbox activities performed by the mailbox owner, a delegated user, or an administrator are automatically logged in the audit log for up to 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-988">管理员可以为组织中的所有用户关闭邮箱审核日志记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-988">It's possible for an admin to turn off mailbox audit logging for all users in your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-989">在这种情况下, ，不会记录任何用户的邮箱操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-989">In this case, no mailbox actions for any user are logged.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-990">有关详细信息，请参阅[管理邮箱审核](enable-mailbox-auditing.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-990">For more information, see [Manage mailbox auditing](enable-mailbox-auditing.md).</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="85d61-991">你还可以使用 Exchange Online PowerShell 中的 [Search-MailboxAuditLog](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/search-mailboxauditlog) cmdlet 来搜索邮箱活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-991">You can also search for mailbox activities by using the [Search-MailboxAuditLog](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/search-mailboxauditlog) cmdlet in Exchange Online PowerShell.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-992">友好名称</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-992">Friendly name</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-993">操作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-993">Operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-994">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-994">Description</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-995">访问的邮箱项目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-995">Accessed mailbox items</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-996">MailItemsAccessed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-996">MailItemsAccessed</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-997">已在邮箱中读取或访问邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-997">Messages were read or accessed in mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-998">此活动的审核记录通过下面两种方式之一触发：当邮箱客户端（如 Outlook）对邮件执行绑定操作时，或者当邮箱客户端（如 Exchange ActiveSync 或 IMAP）同步邮箱文件夹中的项目时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-998">Audit records for this activity are triggered in one of two ways: when a mail client (such as Outlook) performs a bind operation on messages or when mail protocols (such as Exchange ActiveSync or IMAP) sync items in a mail folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-999">仅对具有 Office 365 或 Microsoft 365 E5 许可证的用户记录此活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-999">This activity is only logged for users with an Office 365 or Microsoft 365 E5 license.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1000">调查被盗用的电子邮件帐户时，分析此活动的审核记录非常有用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1000">Analyzing audit records for this activity is useful when investigating compromised email account.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1001">有关详细信息，请参阅 [高级审核](advanced-audit.md#access-to-crucial-events-for-investigations)中的“访问关键事件进行调查”部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1001">For more information, see the "Access to crucial events for investigations" section in [Advanced Audit](advanced-audit.md#access-to-crucial-events-for-investigations).</span></span> |

|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1006">已添加或删除具有日历文件夹代理访问权限的用户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1006">Added or removed user with delegate access to calendar folder</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1007">UpdateCalendarDelegation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1007">UpdateCalendarDelegation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1008">已在其他用户邮箱的日历中添加或删除具有代理身份的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1008">A user was added or removed as a delegate to the calendar of another user's mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1009">日历代理为同一组织内的其他人授予管理邮箱所有者日历的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1009">Calendar delegation gives someone else in the same organization permissions to manage the mailbox owner's calendar.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1051">已删除代理邮箱权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1051">Removed delegate mailbox permissions</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1052">Remove-MailboxPermission</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1052">Remove-MailboxPermission</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1053">管理员已从用户邮箱删除分配给代理的 FullAccess 权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1053">An administrator removed the FullAccess permission (that was assigned to a delegate) from a person's mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1054">删除 FullAccess 权限后，代理无法打开他人邮箱，也无法访问该邮箱中的任何内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1054">After the FullAccess permission is removed, the delegate can't open the other person's mailbox or access any content in it.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1055">已从文件夹中删除权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1055">Removed permissions from folder</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1056">RemoveFolderPermissions</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1056">RemoveFolderPermissions</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1057">已删除文件夹权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1057">A folder permission was removed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1058">文件夹权限用于控制组织中的哪些用户可以访问邮箱中的文件夹以及位于这些文件夹中的邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1058">Folder permissions control which users in your organization can access folders in a mailbox and the messages located in those folders.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1059">已使用“发送方式”权限发送邮件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1059">Sent message using Send As permissions</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1060">SendAs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1060">SendAs</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1061">已使用“发送方式”权限发送邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1061">A message was sent using the SendAs permission.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1062">这表示另一个用户发送了邮件，而该邮件就好像来自于邮箱所有者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1062">This means that another user sent the message as though it came from the mailbox owner.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1071">已更新邮件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1071">Updated message</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1072">更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1072">Update</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1073">已更改邮件或其属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1073">A message or its properties was changed.</span></span>|

### <a name="sway-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-1079">Sway 活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1079">Sway activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1080">下表列出了 Sway 中的用户和管理员活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1080">The following table lists user and admin activities in Sway.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1081">Sway 是一款 Microsoft 365 应用，可帮助用户在基于 Web 的交互式画布上收集、格式化和共享意见、案例和演示文稿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1081">Sway is a Microsoft 365 app that helps users gather, format, and share ideas, stories, and presentations on an interactive, web-based canvas.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1082">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Sway 常见问题 - 管理员帮助](https://support.office.com/article/446380fa-25bf-47b2-996c-e12cb2f9d075)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1082">For more information, see [Frequently asked questions about Sway - Admin Help](https://support.office.com/article/446380fa-25bf-47b2-996c-e12cb2f9d075).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1083">友好名称</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1083">Friendly name</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1084">操作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1084">Operation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1085">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1085">Description</span></span>|

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1279">创建和管理电子数据展示事例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1279">Creating and managing eDiscovery cases</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1293">默认情况下，Power BI 的审核日志记录未启用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1293">Audit logging for Power BI isn't enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1294">若要在审核日志中搜索 Power BI 活动，则必须在 Power BI 管理门户中启用审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1294">To search for Power BI activities in the audit log, you have to enable auditing in the Power BI admin portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1295">有关说明，请参阅 [Power BI 管理门户](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs)中的“审核日志”部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1295">For instructions, see the "Audit logs" section in [Power BI admin portal](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs).</span></span>

### <a name="microsoft-workplace-analytics-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-1296">Microsoft 工作区分析活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1296">Microsoft Workplace Analytics activities</span></span>

#### <a name="forms-activities-performed-by-coauthors-and-anonymous-responders"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-1573">合著者和匿名响应者执行的 Forms 活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1573">Forms activities performed by coauthors and anonymous responders</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1574">Forms 支持在设计表单时和分析响应时进行协作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1574">Forms supports collaboration when forms are being designed and when analyzing responses.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1575">表单协作者被称为*合著者*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1575">A form collaborator is known as a *coauthor*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1576">合著者可执行表单所有者可执行的所有操作，但删除或移动表单除外。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1576">Coauthors can do everything a form owner can do, except delete or move a form.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1577">Forms 还允许你创建可以匿名响应的表单。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1577">Forms also allows you to create a form that can be responded to anonymously.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1578">这意味着响应者无需登录到组织即可响应表单。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1578">This means the responder doesn't have to be signed into your organization to respond to a form.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1579">下表介绍了合著者和匿名响应者执行的活动的审核记录中的审核活动和信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1579">The following table describes the auditing activities and information in the audit record for activities performed by coauthors and anonymous responders.</span></span>

### <a name="exchange-admin-audit-log"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-1675">Exchange 管理员审核日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1675">Exchange admin audit log</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1676">管理员（或已分配有管理权限的用户）在 Exchange Online 组织中做出更改时，Exchange 管理员审核日志记录（Office 365 中默认启用此功能）将在审核日志中记录事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1676">Exchange administrator audit logging (which is enabled by default in Office 365) logs an event in the audit log when an administrator (or a user who has been assigned administrative permissions) makes a change in your Exchange Online organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1677">通过使用 Exchange 管理中心所做的更改或通过运行 Exchange Online PowerShell 中的某个 cmdlet 所做的更改会记录在 Exchange 管理员审核日志中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1677">Changes made by using the Exchange admin center or by running a cmdlet in Exchange Online PowerShell are logged in the Exchange admin audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1678">以动词 **Get-**、**Search-** 或 **Test-** 开头的 Cmdlet 未记录在审核日志中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1678">Cmdlets that begin with the verbs **Get-**, **Search-**, or **Test-** are not logged in the audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1679">有关 Exchange 中管理员审核日志记录的更多详细信息，请参阅[管理员审核日志记录](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=619225)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1679">For more detailed information about admin audit logging in Exchange, see [Administrator audit logging](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=619225).</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1680">某些 Exchange Online cmdlet 未记录在 Exchange 管理员审核日志中（或审核日志中）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1680">Some Exchange Online cmdlets that aren't logged in the Exchange admin audit log (or in the audit log).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1681">其中许多 cmdlet 都与维护 Exchange Online 服务有关，并由 Microsoft 数据中心人员或服务帐户运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1681">Many of these cmdlets are related to maintaining the Exchange Online service and are run by Microsoft datacenter personnel or service accounts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1682">未记录这些 cmdlet，因为它们会导致大量“嘈杂”的审核事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1682">These cmdlets aren't logged because they would result in a large number of "noisy" auditing events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1683">如果存在未经审核的 Exchange Online cmdlet，请向[安全与合规用户之声论坛](https://office365.uservoice.com/forums/289138-office-365-security-compliance)提交建议，并请求进行审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1683">If there's an Exchange Online cmdlet that isn't being audited, please submit a suggestion to the [Security & Compliance User Voice forum](https://office365.uservoice.com/forums/289138-office-365-security-compliance) and request that it is enabled for auditing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1684">你还可以向 Microsoft 支持部门提交设计更改请求 (DCR)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1684">You can also submit a design change request (DCR) to Microsoft Support.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1685">以下是在搜索审核日志时搜索 Exchange 管理员活动的一些提示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1685">Here are some tips for searching for Exchange admin activities when searching the audit log:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1686">若要返回 Exchange 管理员审核日志中的条目，必须选择“**活动**”列表中的“**显示所有活动的结果**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1686">To return entries from the Exchange admin audit log, you have to select **Show results for all activities** in the **Activities** list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1687">使用日期范围框和“**用户**”列表缩小由特定 Exchange 管理员在特定日期范围内运行的 cmdlet 的搜索结果范围。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1687">Use the date range boxes and the **Users** list to narrow the search results for cmdlets run by a specific Exchange administrator within a specific date range.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1688">若要显示 Exchange 管理员审核日志中的事件，请筛选搜索结果并在“**活动**”筛选器框中键入 **-**（破折号）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1688">To display events from the Exchange admin audit log, filter the search results and type a **-** (dash) in the **Activity** filter box.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1689">这将在 Exchange 管理员事件的“**活动**”列中显示 cmdlet 名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1689">This displays cmdlet names, which are displayed in the **Activity** column for Exchange admin events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1690">然后你便可按字母顺序对 cmdlet 名称进行排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1690">Then you can sort the cmdlet names in alphabetical order.</span></span>

  ![在“活动”框中键入一个破折号以筛选 Exchange 管理事件](../media/7628e7aa-6263-474a-a28b-2dcf5694bb27.png)

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1692">若要获取有关已运行的 cmdlet、已使用的参数和参数值以及受影响对象的信息，可以导出搜索结果并选择“**下载所有结果**”选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1692">To get information about what cmdlet was run, which parameters and parameter values were used, and what objects were affected, you can export the search results by selecting the **Download all results** option.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1693">有关详细信息，请参阅[导出、配置和查看审核日志记录](export-view-audit-log-records.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1693">For more information, see [Export, configure, and view audit log records](export-view-audit-log-records.md).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1694">你还可以使用 Exchange Online PowerShell 中的 `Search-UnifiedAuditLog -RecordType ExchangeAdmin` 命令仅从 Exchange 管理员审核日志中返回审核记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1694">You can also use the `Search-UnifiedAuditLog -RecordType ExchangeAdmin` command in Exchange Online PowerShell to return only audit records from the Exchange admin audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1695">运行 Exchange cmdlet 后，可能需要长达 30 分钟的时间在搜索结果中返回相应的审核日志条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1695">It may take up to 30 minutes after an Exchange cmdlet is run for the corresponding audit log entry to be returned in the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1696">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Search-UnifiedAuditLog](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/search-unifiedauditlog)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1696">For more information, see [Search-UnifiedAuditLog](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/search-unifiedauditlog).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1697">有关将 **Search-UnifiedAuditLog** cmdlet 所返回的搜索结果导出到 CSV 文件的信息，请参阅[导出、配置和查看审核日志记录](export-view-audit-log-records.md#tips-for-exporting-and-viewing-the-audit-log)中的“有关导出和查看审核日志的提示”部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1697">For information about exporting the search results returned by the **Search-UnifiedAuditLog** cmdlet to a CSV file, see the "Tips for exporting and viewing the audit log" section in [Export, configure, and view audit log records](export-view-audit-log-records.md#tips-for-exporting-and-viewing-the-audit-log).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1698">你还可以使用 Exchange 管理中心或在 Exchange Online PowerShell 中运行 **Search-AdminAuditLog** 来查看 Exchange 管理员审核日志中的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1698">You can also view events in the Exchange admin audit log by using the Exchange admin center or running the **Search-AdminAuditLog** in Exchange Online PowerShell.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1699">这是一种具体搜索由 Exchange Online 管理员执行的活动的好方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1699">This is a good way to specifically search for activity performed by Exchange Online administrators.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1700">有关说明，请参阅以下内容：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1700">For instructions, see:</span></span>

  - [<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1701">查看管理员审核日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1701">View the administrator audit log</span></span>](https://technet.microsoft.com/library/dn342832%28v=exchg.150%29.aspx)

  - [<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1702">Search-AdminAuditLog</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1702">Search-AdminAuditLog</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/search-adminauditlog)

   <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1703">请注意，Exchange 管理员审核日志以及审核日志中记录了相同的 Exchange 管理员活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1703">Keep in mind that the same Exchange admin activities are logged in both the Exchange admin audit log and audit log.</span></span>

## <a name="frequently-asked-questions"></a><span data-ttu-id="85d61-1704">常见问题解答</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1704">Frequently asked questions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1705">**目前审核的各种 Microsoft 365 服务有哪些？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1705">**What are different Microsoft 365 services that are currently audited?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1706">已审核最常用的服务，例如 Exchange Online、SharePoint Online、OneDrive for Business、Azure Active Directory、Microsoft Teams、Dynamics 365、高级威胁防护和 Power BI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1706">The most used services like Exchange Online, SharePoint Online, OneDrive for Business, Azure Active Directory, Microsoft Teams, Dynamics 365, Advanced Threat Protection, and Power BI are audited.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1707">有关已审核的服务列表，请参阅[本文开头部分](search-the-audit-log-in-security-and-compliance.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1707">See the [beginning of this article](search-the-audit-log-in-security-and-compliance.md) for a list of services that are audited.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1708">**哪些活动由 Office 365 中的审核服务进行审核？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1708">**What activities are audited by auditing service in Office 365?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1709">有关审核的活动列表和说明，请参阅本文[已审核的活动](#audited-activities)部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1709">See the [Audited activities](#audited-activities) section in this article for a list and description of the activities that are audited.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1710">**审核记录在事件发生后的多长时间内可用？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1710">**How long does it take for an auditing record to be available after an event has occurred?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1711">发生事件后，大部分审核数据在 30 分钟内可用，但最长可能需要 24 小时才能在搜索结果中显示相应的审核日志条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1711">Most auditing data is available within 30 minutes but it may take up to 24 hours after an event occurs for the corresponding audit log entry to be displayed in the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1712">请参阅本文[搜索审核日志的要求](#requirements-to-search-the-audit-log)部分中的表，其中显示了各种服务提供事件审核记录所需的时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1712">See the table in the [Requirements to search the audit log](#requirements-to-search-the-audit-log) section of this article that shows the time it takes for events in the different services to be available.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1713">**审核记录将保留多长时间？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1713">**How long are the audit records retained for?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1714">正如前面所述，分配了 Office 365 E5 或 Microsoft E5 许可证的用户（或者拥有 Microsoft 365 E5 附加许可证的用户）所执行活动的审核记录将保留一年。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1714">As previously explained, audit records for activities performed by users assigned an Office 365 E5 or Microsoft E5 license (or users with a Microsoft 365 E5 add-on license) are retained for one year.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1715">对于支持统一审核日志记录的所有其他订阅，审核记录将保留 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1715">For all other subscriptions that support unified audit logging, audit records are retained for 90 days.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1716">**我是否可以通过编程方式访问审核数据？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1716">**Can I access the auditing data programmatically?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1717">是。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1717">Yes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1718">Office 365 管理活动 API 用于以编程方式获取审核日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1718">The Office 365 Management Activity API is used to fetch the audit logs programmatically.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1719">若要开始使用，请参阅 [Office 365 管理 API 入门](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/office-365-management-api/get-started-with-office-365-management-apis)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1719">To get started, see [Get started with Office 365 Management APIs](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/office-365-management-api/get-started-with-office-365-management-apis).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1720">**除了使用安全与合规中心或 Office 365 管理活动 API 之外，是否还有其他方法可以获取审核日志？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1720">**Are there other ways to get auditing logs other than using the security and compliance center or the Office 365 Management Activity API?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1721">不正确。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1721">No.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1722">以下是从审核服务获取数据的两种方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1722">These are the only two ways to get data from the auditing service.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1723">**是否需要在每个要捕获审核日志的服务中单独启用审核？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1723">**Do I need to individually enable auditing in each service that I want to capture audit logs for?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1724">在大多数服务中，在首次为组织启用审核后将默认启用审核功能（如本文[搜索审核日志的要求](#requirements-to-search-the-audit-log)部分所述）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1724">In most services, auditing is enabled by default after you initially turn on auditing for your organization (as described in the [Requirements to search the audit log](#requirements-to-search-the-audit-log) section in this article).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1725">**审核服务是否支持记录的重复数据删除？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1725">**Does the auditing service support de-duplication of records?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1726">不正确。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1726">No.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1727">审核服务管道几乎是实时的，因此不能支持重复数据删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1727">The auditing service pipeline is near real time, and therefore can't support de-duplication.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1728">**审核数据是否跨地域流动？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1728">**Does auditing data flow across geographies?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1729">不正确。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1729">No.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1730">我们目前在 NA（北美）、EMEA（欧洲、中东和非洲）和 APAC（亚太地区）进行了审核管道部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1730">We currently have auditing pipeline deployments in the NA (North America), EMEA (Europe, Middle East, and Africa) and APAC (Asia Pacific) regions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1731">但是，我们可能会使数据跨这些区域流动以实现负载平衡，并且仅在现场出现问题时才会这样做。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1731">However, we may flow the data across these regions for load-balancing and only during live-site issues.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1732">当我们执行这些活动时，传输中的数据会被加密。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1732">When we do perform these activities, the data in transit is encrypted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1733">**审核数据是否已加密？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1733">**Is auditing data encrypted?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1734">审核数据存储在部署统一审核管道的同一区域内的 Exchange 邮箱中（静态数据）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1734">Auditing data is stored in Exchange mailboxes (data at rest) in the same region where the unified auditing pipeline is deployed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1735">Exchange 不会对邮箱静态数据加密。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1735">Mailbox data at rest is not encrypted by Exchange.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1736">但是，服务级加密将对所有邮箱数据进行加密，因为 Microsoft 数据中心内的 Exchange 服务器将通过 BitLocker 加密。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1736">However, service-level encryption encrypts all mailbox data because Exchange servers in Microsoft datacenters are encrypted via BitLocker.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="85d61-1737">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Skype for Business、OneDrive for Business、SharePoint Online 和 Exchange Online 的 Office 365 加密](office-365-encryption-for-skype-onedrive-sharepoint-and-exchange.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1737">For more information, see [Office 365 Encryption for Skype for Business, OneDrive for Business, SharePoint Online, and Exchange Online](office-365-encryption-for-skype-onedrive-sharepoint-and-exchange.md).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="85d61-1738">传输中的数据始终是加密的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="85d61-1738">Mail data in transit is always encrypted.</span></span>
